 jisase beej or khaad ab nahin diya ja saktaa he

 Only able to work for 2 to 30 hours

 40 or 50 ke dashak main apane kaam kaa loha manwaane vaale ashok kumaar kaa aaj janmdin he
 Ashok Kumar used to practice painter and homeopathy along with an acting
 ashok kumaarane 'achhut kanya', 'haavda brij', 'kismat', 'aashirwad', 'sangram', 'samadhi', 'bandini', 'chitralekha', 'jevel thief', 'pakija', 'choti si baat', 'khubasurat', 'mili' jaisi behtareen filmon main kaam kiya
 He has also worked in more than 275 films and more than 30 Bengali dramas
 aaie ashok kumaar sahab ke bare main jaanate hai kuch khaas baaten
 1
 ashok kumaar kaa janm 13 oktober1911 ko bhagalpur bihar main hua tha
 2
 janm ke vakt inkaa naam 'kumudlal ganguli' tha or film industry main pyaar se log inhen 'dadamuni (bada bhai)' bhi kehete the
 3
 ashok kumaarake pita kunjalaal ganguli ek vakil the or unki maa gharelu mahila thi
 Ashok was a big boy in the house followed by his sister Sati Devi, then brothers Kishore Kumar and Anup Kumar
 4
 Ashok Kumar had a dream of working in the film industry since childhood, but not as an actor but as a technician
 5
 In those days, Ashok Kumar's brother-in-law Sashadhar Mukherjee used to work in a high position in 'bombay Talkies' in Mumbai, due to which Ashok Kumar moved to Mumbai and started working as a 'lab Assistant' in Bombay Talkies itself
 6
 Even before the shooting of 'jeevan Naiya', a film made under the Bombay Talkies of 1936, there were differences between its lead actors Devika Rani and Najmul Hasan, due to which the producer of the film Himanshu Rai replaced Najmul with Kumudlal (ashok Kumar) was called in the film, although the director of the film was unhappy about this, but Himanshu took him into the film and for the first time, Kumudlal Ganguly's screen Program 'ashok Kumar has put' because those days Actors his real name was not revealed on the screen
 7
 Then along with Devika Rani, Ashok Kumar also did films like 'untouchable Girl' of 1936 followed by 'janmabhoomi', 'izzat', 'savitri', 'vyakha', and 'nirmala'
 8
 In those days in the 40s, Ashok Kumar did films like 'kangan', 'bandhan', 'azad' and 'jhoola' with actress 'leela Chitnis', and after Jhula, Ashok Kumar became the most trusted star of the film industry
 9
 The 1943 film 'kismet' broke all the box office records in those days and became the first film in the Hindi film industry to cross the Rs 1 crore mark and became Ashok Kumar 'superstar' overnight
 10
 In 1988, Ashok Kumar was awarded the 'dadasaheb Phalke' Award and in 1998 was awarded the 'padma Bhushan'

 in imaaraton se jude fact:dharhara tower :1
 Nepal's tallest Dharahara tower, also known as Qutub Minar, has been destroyed by the disaster on April 25
 2

 3

 4
 The steps in this building were made in spiral shape

 Kathmandu's finest views were seen from the eighth floor of the building
